                  <form>       
                     <orth orig="" extent="full" lang="ar">مَوْصُولٌ</orth>
                     <orth extent="full" lang="ar">ذ</orth>
                  </form>, in grammar, [<hi rend="ital">A conjunct</hi>]. This is of two kinds; <foreign lang="ar">مَوْصُولٌ حَرْفِىٌّ</foreign> and <foreign lang="ar">مَوْصُولٌ إِسْمِىٌّ</foreign>. The former term [or <hi rend="ital">conjunct particle</hi>] is applied to the infinitive particles <foreign lang="ar">أَنْ</foreign>, <foreign lang="ar">أَنَّ</foreign>, <foreign lang="ar">كَى</foreign>, <foreign lang="ar">لَوْ</foreign>, and <foreign lang="ar">مَا</foreign>. The latter term [or <hi rend="ital">conjunct noun</hi>] (I have thus rendered it voce <foreign lang="ar">أَلْ</foreign>, and voce <foreign lang="ar">إِنْ</foreign>, and voce <foreign lang="ar">إِنَّ</foreign>) is applied to the conjunctive nouns <foreign lang="ar">أَلَّذِى</foreign>, and its fem. <foreign lang="ar">اَلَّتِى</foreign>, and <foreign lang="ar">مَنْ</foreign>, and <foreign lang="ar">مَا</foreign>, and <foreign lang="ar">ذُو</foreign> in the dial. of Teiyi, and to <foreign lang="ar">اَلْ</foreign>, which last some incorrectly hold to be a conjunct particle, and others assert to be a determinative particle and not a conjunct, and to <foreign lang="ar">ذَا</foreign> after the interrogative <foreign lang="ar">مَا</foreign> or <foreign lang="ar">مَنْ</foreign>.
